 #!/usr/bin/env bash
 # Build, sign, notarize, staple, and upload a Plow DMG.
 set -euo pipefail
 
 usage() {
   cat <<'EOF'
 Usage: plowd-beta-package-signed [options]
 
 Options:
   --app-bundle <path>       Built Plow.app bundle to package
   --output <path>           Output DMG path
   --entitlements <path>     Entitlements plist for the top-level app signature
   --identity <value>        Developer ID Application signing identity
   --notary-profile <name>   notarytool keychain profile name
   --s3-bucket <name>        S3 bucket for upload
   --release-prefix <path>   Optional S3 prefix for versioned release artifacts
   --s3-profile <name>       AWS profile name
   --sparkle-account <name>  Sparkle keychain account name for generate_appcast
   -h, --help                Show this help
 
 Environment:
   PLOW_CODESIGN_IDENTITY    Default signing identity if --identity is omitted
   PLOW_APPLE_TEAM_ID        Apple team id for identity auto-detection
   PLOW_NOTARY_PROFILE       Default notary profile if --notary-profile is omitted
   PLOW_RELEASES_BUCKET      Default S3 bucket (default: releases.plow.co)
   PLOW_RELEASES_PROFILE     Default AWS profile (default: plow)
   PLOW_SPARKLE_ACCOUNT      Default Sparkle key account (default: plow-sparkle)
   PLOW_KEEP_SIGNED_APP      When set to 1, keep a copy of the signed app at .build/Plow-signed.app
 EOF
 }
 
 repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
 validate_script="${repo_root}/app/plowd/scripts/plowd-validate-package"
 stage_sparkle_script="${repo_root}/app/plowd/scripts/plowd-stage-sparkle-feed"
 publish_sparkle_script="${repo_root}/app/plowd/scripts/plowd-publish-sparkle-feed"
 dmg_assets_dir="${repo_root}/app/plowd/dmg"
+dmg_ds_store="${dmg_assets_dir}/.DS_Store"
 dmg_background="${dmg_assets_dir}/background.tiff"
-dmg_volume_icon="${dmg_assets_dir}/volume.icns"
 app_bundle="${repo_root}/.build/xcode-derived/Build/Products/Release/Plow.app"
 output="${repo_root}/.build/Plow.dmg"
 entitlements="${repo_root}/app/Phoenix/Phoenix.entitlements"
 limactl_entitlements="${repo_root}/app/Phoenix/Limactl.entitlements"
 identity="${PLOW_CODESIGN_IDENTITY:-}"
 team_id="${PLOW_APPLE_TEAM_ID:-3559PD337Z}"
 notary_profile="${PLOW_NOTARY_PROFILE:-plow-notary}"
 s3_bucket="${PLOW_RELEASES_BUCKET:-releases.plow.co}"
 release_prefix=""
 s3_profile="${PLOW_RELEASES_PROFILE:-plow}"
 sparkle_account="${PLOW_SPARKLE_ACCOUNT:-plow-sparkle}"
 keep_signed_app="${PLOW_KEEP_SIGNED_APP:-0}"
 
 while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
   case "$1" in
     --app-bundle)
       app_bundle="${2:-}"
       shift 2
       ;;
     --output)
       output="${2:-}"
       shift 2
       ;;
     --entitlements)
       entitlements="${2:-}"
       shift 2
       ;;
     --identity)
       identity="${2:-}"
       shift 2
       ;;
     --notary-profile)
       notary_profile="${2:-}"
       shift 2
       ;;
     --s3-bucket)
       s3_bucket="${2:-}"
       shift 2
       ;;
     --release-prefix)
       release_prefix="${2:-}"
       shift 2
       ;;
     --s3-profile)
       s3_profile="${2:-}"
       shift 2
       ;;
     --sparkle-account)
       sparkle_account="${2:-}"
       shift 2
       ;;
     -h|--help)
       usage
       exit 0
       ;;
     *)
       echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
       usage >&2
       exit 1
       ;;
   esac
 done
 
 resolve_path() {
   local path="$1"
   if [[ "${path}" = /* ]]; then
     echo "${path}"
   else
     echo "${repo_root}/${path}"
   fi
 }
 
 plist_read() {
     local plist_path="$1"
     local key="$2"
     /usr/bin/python3 -c "
 import plistlib, sys
 try:
     with open(sys.argv[1], 'rb') as f:
         d = plistlib.load(f)
     print(d.get(sys.argv[2], ''), end='')
 except Exception:
     pass
 " "${plist_path}" "${key}" 2>/dev/null || true
 }
 
 ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume() {
   local mounted_plow_volumes
   mounted_plow_volumes="$(
     hdiutil info 2>/dev/null \
       | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true
   )"
   mounted_plow_volumes="$(
     printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" \
       | sort -u
   )"
   [[ -z "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]] && return
 
   echo "error: a Plow disk image is already mounted; eject it before packaging:" >&2
   printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
   exit 1
 }
 
 app_bundle="$(resolve_path "${app_bundle}")"
 output="$(resolve_path "${output}")"
 entitlements="$(resolve_path "${entitlements}")"
 limactl_entitlements="$(resolve_path "${limactl_entitlements}")"
 
 if [[ -z "${identity}" ]]; then
   [[ -n "${team_id}" ]] || { echo "error: PLOW_APPLE_TEAM_ID is required when --identity is not provided" >&2; exit 1; }
   identity="$(security find-identity -v -p codesigning 2>/dev/null | sed -n "s/.*\"\\(Developer ID Application:.*(${team_id})\\)\"/\\1/p" | head -n 1)"
 fi
 
 [[ -n "${identity}" ]] || { echo "error: no Developer ID Application identity found for team ${team_id}; install one for that team before running release" >&2; exit 1; }
 if [[ -n "${team_id}" && "${identity}" != *"(${team_id})"* ]]; then
   echo "error: selected signing identity does not match required Apple team ${team_id}: ${identity}" >&2
   exit 1
 fi
 [[ -d "${app_bundle}" ]] || { echo "error: app bundle not found: ${app_bundle}" >&2; exit 1; }
 [[ -f "${entitlements}" ]] || { echo "error: entitlements file not found: ${entitlements}" >&2; exit 1; }
 [[ -f "${limactl_entitlements}" ]] || { echo "error: limactl entitlements file not found: ${limactl_entitlements}" >&2; exit 1; }
 [[ -x "${validate_script}" ]] || { echo "error: package validator not found: ${validate_script}" >&2; exit 1; }

     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	#
     3	# Interactively record the Finder window layout for the release DMG.
     4	#
     5	# Why this script exists
     6	# ----------------------
     7	# When the user double-clicks the released .dmg, Finder opens the volume
     8	# in a window with a custom background image, hidden toolbar/sidebar,
     9	# and Plow.app + Applications icons in fixed positions. None of that
    10	# styling can be set programmatically by hdiutil — Finder reads it from
    11	# a .DS_Store at the volume root. We used to set up that .DS_Store with
    12	# AppleScript at packaging time, but that automation was flaky in CI and
    13	# was removed in favor of shipping a pre-recorded .DS_Store checked in
    14	# at app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store. plowd-beta-package-signed ditto's that
    15	# file into the staging dir before hdiutil create. So: edits to the
    16	# install-window appearance must be made by re-running this script and
    17	# committing the resulting .DS_Store.
    18	#
    19	# How it works
    20	# ------------
    21	# 1. Stage the same files plowd-beta-package-signed ships: Plow.app,
    22	#    Applications symlink, .background/background.tiff.
    23	# 2. Create a writable (UDRW) DMG and mount it. Finder pops open the
    24	#    volume window; the user arranges it (View Options for background,
    25	#    icon size, arrangement; drag for icon positions and window size).
    26	# 3. User closes the window (Cmd-W), which prompts Finder to flush
    27	#    .DS_Store, and presses Enter at the script's prompt.
    28	# 4. Eject and re-mount. The eject is what guarantees Finder has
    29	#    written .DS_Store to disk; reading it from a still-mounted volume
    30	#    can return a stale or empty file.
    31	# 5. Copy /Volumes/Plow/.DS_Store -> app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store and
    32	#    detach.
    33	#
    34	# Display-size caveat
    35	# -------------------
    36	# .DS_Store stores the install window's bounds as absolute screen
    37	# coordinates relative to the main display. If you record on a large
    38	# display with the window at (e.g.) 2000,1500, Finder on a small
    39	# laptop will reposition the off-screen window to fit, which loses
    40	# your placement. Record near the top-left of your screen and keep the
    41	# window modest (~680x420 fits every Mac display).
    42	#
    43	# Verifying after recording
    44	# -------------------------
    45	# Before committing, build a release DMG (or stage by hand and run
    46	# hdiutil create -format ULFO with the new .DS_Store ditto'd in) and
    47	# open it to confirm Finder honors the layout. The captured .DS_Store
    48	# should grow noticeably (~6 KB+) when a background picture is set;
    49	# a near-8 KB unchanged size suggests the picture didn't take.
    50	#
    51	# Why a separate script (vs inline in plowd-beta-package-signed)
    52	# --------------------------------------------------------------
    53	# This is a one-off authoring tool with mandatory human-in-Finder
    54	# steps; the release script is unattended CI. Keeping them separate
    55	# makes the release path deterministic (just `ditto` a checked-in
    56	# blob) and lets layout changes go through a normal code review of
    57	# the .DS_Store diff.
    58	set -euo pipefail
    59	
    60	usage() {
    61	  cat <<'EOF'
    62	Usage: plowd-record-dmg-layout [--app <path>]
    63	
    64	Records app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store from an interactive Finder layout
    65	session. Mounts a writable scratch DMG that mirrors the staging
    66	plowd-beta-package-signed ships, drops you into Finder to arrange the
    67	install window, then captures the resulting .DS_Store back into the
    68	repo when you press Enter at the prompt.
    69	
    70	Workflow once mounted at /Volumes/Plow:
    71	  1. View > as Icons (Cmd-1)
    72	  2. View > Hide Toolbar (Opt-Cmd-T)
    73	  3. View > Show View Options (Cmd-J)
    74	       - size/position the window (keep it under ~680x420 and near
    75	         the top-left of your screen so it fits on small displays)
    76	       - drag .background/background.tiff into Background > Picture
    77	         (open a second Finder window, Cmd-Shift-. to show hidden
    78	         files, then drag the .tiff into the well; the file picker
    79	         is unreliable for hidden paths)
    80	       - icon size, text size, arrangement = None
    81	  4. Drag Plow.app and Applications icons into position
    82	  5. Close the volume window (Cmd-W) to flush .DS_Store
    83	  6. Press Enter at this script's prompt to capture
    84	
    85	Options:
    86	  --app <path>   Path to the .app to stage. Defaults to the release
    87	                 build at .build/xcode-derived/Build/Products/Release/
    88	                 Plow.app, falling back to /Applications/Plow.app
    89	                 (which is fine for layout-only iteration since icon
    90	                 positions are recorded by filename).
    91	  -h, --help     Show this message.
    92	EOF
    93	}
    94	
    95	repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
    96	app_path=""
    97	
    98	while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
    99	  case "$1" in
   100	    --app)
   101	      app_path="${2:-}"
   102	      shift 2
   103	      ;;
   104	    -h|--help)
   105	      usage
   106	      exit 0
   107	      ;;
   108	    *)
   109	      echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
   110	      usage >&2
   111	      exit 1
   112	      ;;
   113	  esac
   114	done
   115	
   116	if [[ -z "${app_path}" ]]; then
   117	  release_app="${repo_root}/.build/xcode-derived/Build/Products/Release/Plow.app"
   118	  if [[ -d "${release_app}" ]]; then
   119	    app_path="${release_app}"
   120	  elif [[ -d "/Applications/Plow.app" ]]; then
   121	    app_path="/Applications/Plow.app"
   122	    echo "note: using /Applications/Plow.app (no release build found)"
   123	  else
   124	    echo "error: no Plow.app found; pass --app <path>, run 'just app release', or install via /plow-prod-install" >&2
   125	    exit 1
   126	  fi
   127	fi

   129

   133

   135	mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
   136	if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then

   138	  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
   139	  exit 1
   140	fi
   141	
   142	work_dir="$(mktemp -d /tmp/plowd-dmg-record.XXXXXX)"
   143	stage_dir="${work_dir}/stage"
   144	rw_dmg="${work_dir}/layout.dmg"
   145	mounted_volume=""
   146	cleanup() {

   149	  fi
   150	  rm -rf "${work_dir}"

   152	trap cleanup EXIT
   153	
   154	mkdir -p "${stage_dir}/.background"
   155	ditto "${app_path}" "${stage_dir}/Plow.app"
   156	ditto "${bg_src}" "${stage_dir}/.background/background.tiff"
   157	ln -s /Applications "${stage_dir}/Applications"

   159	hdiutil create -volname "Plow" -srcfolder "${stage_dir}" -ov -format UDRW "${rw_dmg}" >/dev/null

   167	
   168	In Finder:
   169	  - View > as Icons (Cmd-1)
   170	  - View > Hide Toolbar (Opt-Cmd-T)
   171	  - View > Show View Options (Cmd-J)
   172	      * size/position the window
   173	      * drag .background/background.tiff into Background > Picture
   174	        (Cmd-Shift-. in the picker shows hidden files)
   175	      * set icon size, text size, arrangement = None

+#!/usr/bin/env bash
+# Mount a Plow DMG and assert it has no custom volume icon (PLO-29 regression
+# guard) and that the volume name is "Plow". Detaches before exiting.
+set -euo pipefail
+
+usage() {
+  cat <<'EOF'
+Usage: plowd-verify-dmg [<dmg-path>]
+
+Mounts the given DMG, asserts the mounted volume is named "Plow" and has no
+.VolumeIcon.icns at its root, then detaches. With no argument, defaults to
+.build/Plow.dmg relative to the repo root. A relative argument is resolved
+against the repo root.
+EOF
+}
+
+repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
+default_dmg=".build/Plow.dmg"
+
+dmg_path=""
+case "${1:-}" in
+  -h|--help)
+    usage
+    exit 0
+    ;;
+  "")
+    dmg_path="${repo_root}/${default_dmg}"
+    ;;
+  -*)
+    echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
+    usage >&2
+    exit 1
+    ;;
+  *)
+    dmg_path="$1"
+    if (( $# > 1 )); then
+      echo "error: unexpected extra arguments: ${*:2}" >&2
+      usage >&2
+      exit 1
+    fi
+    ;;
+esac
+
+if [[ "${dmg_path}" != /* ]]; then
+  dmg_path="${repo_root}/${dmg_path}"
+fi
+
+[[ -f "${dmg_path}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG not found: ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+# Refuse to run when a Plow volume is already mounted: the new mountpoint
+# would be "Plow 1" / "Plow 2" / ..., which would mask a real regression in
+# the volume-name assertion below.
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
+if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
+  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before verifying:" >&2
+  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
+  exit 1
+fi
+
+mounted_volume=""
+cleanup() {
+  local rc=$?
+  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
+    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
+      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
+      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
+      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
+      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
+        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
+        exit 1
+      fi
+    else
+      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
+      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
+    fi
+  fi
+  exit "${rc}"
+}
+trap cleanup EXIT
+
+attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${dmg_path}" -nobrowse -readonly)"
+# Real `hdiutil attach` prints one line per partition; the data partition's
+# last whitespace-delimited field is the mount point. Other lines (e.g. the
+# GUID partition scheme) end in a partition-type token that doesn't start
+# with "/". Pick the last line whose final field is an absolute path —
+# works for both real hdiutil's multi-line tabular output and a single-line
+# stub.
+mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | awk '$NF ~ /^\// { last=$NF } END { print last }')"
+[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to mount ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+volume_name="$(basename "${mounted_volume}")"
+[[ "${volume_name}" == "Plow" ]] || { echo "error: mounted volume name is '${volume_name}', expected 'Plow'" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+[[ ! -e "${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns" ]] || {
+  echo "error: ${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns exists; PLO-29 regression: DMG ships a custom volume icon" >&2
+  exit 1
+}
+
+echo "ok: ${dmg_path} mounts as 'Plow' with no custom volume icon"

    56	  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before verifying:" >&2
    57	  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
    58	  exit 1
    59	fi
    60	
    61	mounted_volume=""
    62	cleanup() {
    63	  local rc=$?
    64	  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
    65	    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
    66	      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
    67	      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
    68	      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
    69	      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
    70	        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
    71	        exit 1
    72	      fi
    73	    else
    74	      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
    75	      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    76	    fi
    77	  fi
    78	  exit "${rc}"
    79	}
    80	trap cleanup EXIT
    81	
    82	attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${dmg_path}" -nobrowse -readonly)"
    83	# Real `hdiutil attach` prints one line per partition; the data partition's
    84	# last whitespace-delimited field is the mount point. Other lines (e.g. the
    85	# GUID partition scheme) end in a partition-type token that doesn't start
    86	# with "/". Pick the last line whose final field is an absolute path —
    87	# works for both real hdiutil's multi-line tabular output and a single-line
    88	# stub.
    89	mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | awk '$NF ~ /^\// { last=$NF } END { print last }')"
    90	[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to mount ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
    91	
    92	volume_name="$(basename "${mounted_volume}")"
    93	[[ "${volume_name}" == "Plow" ]] || { echo "error: mounted volume name is '${volume_name}', expected 'Plow'" >&2; exit 1; }
    94	
    95	[[ ! -e "${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns" ]] || {
    96	  echo "error: ${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns exists; PLO-29 regression: DMG ships a custom volume icon" >&2
    97	  exit 1
    98	}
    99	
   100	echo "ok: ${dmg_path} mounts as 'Plow' with no custom volume icon"

 def _provision_fake_bin(fake_bin: Path, systemctl_log: Path) -> None:
     """Write stub commands sufficient to run provision-runtime.sh on macOS."""
     stubs = {
         # zstd just needs to be on PATH so the apt-get install branch is skipped
         "zstd": "#!/bin/sh\n",
         # sha256sum: hash stdin or file args, mimicking GNU coreutils behaviour
         "sha256sum": textwrap.dedent("""\
             #!/usr/bin/env python3
             import hashlib, sys
             from pathlib import Path
             args = [a for a in sys.argv[1:] if a != "--"]
             if args:
                 for arg in args:
                     try:
                         data = Path(arg).read_bytes()
                         print(hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest() + "  " + arg)
                     except FileNotFoundError:
                         print(f"sha256sum: {arg}: No such file or directory", file=sys.stderr)
                         sys.exit(1)
             else:
                 data = sys.stdin.buffer.read()
                 print(hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest() + "  -")
             """),
         # systemctl: log every invocation; always succeed
         "systemctl": f'#!/bin/sh\necho "$@" >> "{systemctl_log}"\n',
     }
     for name, body in stubs.items():
         p = fake_bin / name
         p.write_text(body)
         p.chmod(0o755)
 
 
 def _run_provision(tmp_path: Path, fake_bin: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
     unit_dir = tmp_path / "units"
     unit_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
     libexec_dir = tmp_path / "libexec"
     libexec_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
     bin_dir = tmp_path / "usr-local-bin"
     bin_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
     runtime_env_dir = tmp_path / "runtimes"
     runtime_env_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
     return subprocess.run(
         ["bash", str(PROVISION_SCRIPT)],
         capture_output=True,
         text=True,
         env={
             **subprocess.os.environ,
             "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
             "PLOW_UNIT_DIR": str(unit_dir),
             "PLOW_LIBEXEC_DIR": str(libexec_dir),
             "PLOW_BIN_DIR": str(bin_dir),
             "PLOW_RUNTIME_ENV_DIR": str(runtime_env_dir),
         },
     )
 
 
 def _dry_run_dispatcher(dispatcher: Path, env_file: Path) -> list[str]:
     result = subprocess.run(
         ["bash", str(dispatcher)],
         capture_output=True,
         text=True,
         env={
             **subprocess.os.environ,
             "PLOW_RUNTIME_ENV_FILE": str(env_file),
             "PLOW_RUNTIME_DRY_RUN": "1",
         },
     )
     assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
     return result.stdout.splitlines()

 def test_git_ref_script_defaults_to_parent_commit_for_stable_rebuilds(tmp_path):
     repo_root = tmp_path / "repo"
     repo_root.mkdir()
 
     def git(*args: str) -> str:
         result = subprocess.run(
             ["git", *args],
             capture_output=True,
             text=True,
             cwd=repo_root,
             check=True,
         )
         return result.stdout.strip()
 
     git("init")
     git("config", "user.name", "Test User")
     git("config", "user.email", "test@example.com")
 
     tracked_file = repo_root / "tracked.txt"
     tracked_file.write_text("first\n", encoding="utf-8")
     git("add", "tracked.txt")
     git("commit", "-m", "first")
     parent_ref = git("rev-parse", "--short=7", "HEAD")
 
     tracked_file.write_text("second\n", encoding="utf-8")
     git("commit", "-am", "second")
 
     result = subprocess.run(
         [
             "bash",
             "-lc",
             'source "$1"; REPO_ROOT="$2"; compute_git_ref',
             "bash",
             str(GIT_REF_SCRIPT),
             str(repo_root),
         ],
         capture_output=True,
         text=True,
         cwd=REPO_ROOT,
     )
 
     assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
     assert result.stdout.strip() == parent_ref

+@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
+def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_dmg_shipping_volume_icon(tmp_path):
+    """PLO-29 artifact-level guard. Catches the failure mode that
+    ``test_signed_package_script_stages_release_dmg_contents`` cannot:
+    a regression that re-attaches the DMG post-``hdiutil create``
+    and re-stages a custom volume icon at the final-image stage. We build
+    three real DMGs with hdiutil and assert plowd-verify-dmg accepts the
+    clean one and rejects each regression shape.
+
+    plowd-verify-dmg is wired into plowd-beta-package-signed between staple
+    and S3 upload, so a rejection here aborts ``just release`` before any
+    artifact ships."""
+    # Refuse to run if a real Plow volume is already mounted: the script
+    # bails on that and our assertions would tag the wrong failure mode.
+    info = subprocess.run(
+        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
+    )
+    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
+        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
+
+    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
+    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
+    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
+
+    def make_dmg(dmg_path: Path, *, volname: str) -> None:
+        subprocess.run(
+            [
+                "hdiutil", "create",
+                "-volname", volname,
+                "-srcfolder", str(stage),
+                "-ov",
+                "-format", "ULFO",
+                str(dmg_path),
+            ],
+            check=True, capture_output=True,
+        )
+
+    def run_verify(dmg_path: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
+        return subprocess.run(
+            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), str(dmg_path)],
+            capture_output=True, text=True,
+        )
+
+    # Happy path: clean Plow DMG with no .VolumeIcon must pass.
+    clean_dmg = tmp_path / "clean.dmg"
+    make_dmg(clean_dmg, volname="Plow")
+    ok = run_verify(clean_dmg)
+    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"clean DMG rejected: stdout={ok.stdout!r} stderr={ok.stderr!r}"
+
+    # Regression #1: someone re-introduces .VolumeIcon.icns at the volume root.
+    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_text("fake-icns")
+    iconed_dmg = tmp_path / "iconed.dmg"
+    make_dmg(iconed_dmg, volname="Plow")
+    fail = run_verify(iconed_dmg)
+    assert fail.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns"
+    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in fail.stderr
+
+    # Regression #2: someone parameterizes -volname to something other than "Plow".
+    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").unlink()
+    misnamed_dmg = tmp_path / "misnamed.dmg"
+    make_dmg(misnamed_dmg, volname="NotPlow")
+    fail2 = run_verify(misnamed_dmg)
+    assert fail2.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG with wrong volume name"
+    assert "expected 'Plow'" in fail2.stderr
+
+

+def test_plowd_verify_dmg_propagates_detach_failure_on_success_path(tmp_path):
+    """Round-2: if `hdiutil detach` fails on the success path (e.g. the
+    volume is busy), plowd-verify-dmg must exit non-zero. The previous
+    `|| true` swallowed the failure and returned 0, leaking /Volumes/Plow,
+    which then tripped ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume on the next release
+    retry. This test injects an `hdiutil` wrapper whose `detach` always
+    fails and asserts the script surfaces it."""

+        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
+    )

+        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
+

+    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
+    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
+    subprocess.run(
+        [
+            "hdiutil", "create",
+            "-volname", "Plow",
+            "-srcfolder", str(stage),
+            "-ov",
+            "-format", "ULFO",
+            str(dmg),
+        ],
+        check=True, capture_output=True,
+    )
+
+    real_hdiutil = subprocess.run(

 succeeded in 0ms:
+    real_hdiutil = subprocess.run(
+        ["which", "hdiutil"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
+    ).stdout.strip()
+    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
+    fake_bin.mkdir()
+    wrapper = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
+    wrapper.write_text(

+        f'if [[ "$1" == "detach" ]]; then\n'

+            f"expected 'failed to detach' in stderr, got: {result.stderr!r}"

+        subprocess.run(

+# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
+# Cross-platform verifier tests. These drive plowd-verify-dmg through a fake
+# `hdiutil` that points the verifier at a tmp directory whose contents and
+# basename the test controls. They exercise the same accept/reject code path
+# the real release run takes — no env-skip, no green skip — so the verifier's
+# decision logic is covered on every CI lane (including non-macOS ones that
+# can't run real hdiutil at all).
+# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
+def _write_verifier_fake_hdiutil(fake_bin: Path, mount_path: Path) -> None:
+    """Stub `hdiutil` so plowd-verify-dmg attaches to ``mount_path``.
+
+    The verifier shells out to `hdiutil info` (mount listing), `hdiutil
+    attach` (which prints a tabular line whose final column is the mount
+    point) and `hdiutil detach` on cleanup. The stub:
+
+    - prints nothing for `info` (no /Volumes/Plow already mounted)
+    - prints `/dev/disk9s1 Apple_APFS <mount_path>` for `attach`
+    - succeeds for `detach`
+
+    The test pre-stages ``mount_path`` with whatever contents and basename
+    it wants the verifier to see.
+    """
+    fake_bin.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
+    hdiutil = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
+    hdiutil.write_text(
+        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
+        "case \"$1\" in\n"
+        "  info) exit 0 ;;\n"
+        f"  attach) printf '/dev/disk9s1 Apple_APFS %s\\n' '{mount_path}'; exit 0 ;;\n"
+        "  detach) exit 0 ;;\n"
+        "  *) exit 1 ;;\n"
+        "esac\n"
+    )
+    hdiutil.chmod(0o755)
+
+
+def _run_verifier_with_fake_hdiutil(
+    tmp_path: Path,
+    *,
+    mount_basename: str,
+    stage_volume_icon: bool,
+) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
+    """Stage a fake mount + DMG file, run plowd-verify-dmg, return result."""
+    mount_path = tmp_path / "fake-mount" / mount_basename
+    mount_path.mkdir(parents=True)
+    if stage_volume_icon:
+        (mount_path / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_bytes(b"fake-icns")
+    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
+    _write_verifier_fake_hdiutil(fake_bin, mount_path)
+    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
+    dmg.write_bytes(b"fake-dmg")
+    return subprocess.run(
+        [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), str(dmg)],
+        capture_output=True,
+        text=True,
+        env={
+            **subprocess.os.environ,
+            "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
+        },
+    )
+
+
+def test_plowd_verify_dmg_accepts_clean_mount_via_fake_hdiutil(tmp_path):
+    """Happy path: mount basename is 'Plow' and no .VolumeIcon.icns at root.
+    The verifier must accept and exit 0 — no env skip required."""
+    result = _run_verifier_with_fake_hdiutil(
+        tmp_path, mount_basename="Plow", stage_volume_icon=False,
+    )
+    assert result.returncode == 0, (
+        f"clean mount rejected: stdout={result.stdout!r} stderr={result.stderr!r}"
+    )
+    assert "ok:" in result.stdout
+
+
+def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_volume_icon_via_fake_hdiutil(tmp_path):
+    """The verifier must reject when .VolumeIcon.icns exists at the mount
+    root — that is the PLO-29 regression shape it exists to catch."""
+    result = _run_verifier_with_fake_hdiutil(
+        tmp_path, mount_basename="Plow", stage_volume_icon=True,
+    )
+    assert result.returncode != 0, (
+        f"verifier accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns: "
+        f"stdout={result.stdout!r} stderr={result.stderr!r}"
+    )
+    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in result.stderr
+
+
+def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_wrong_volname_via_fake_hdiutil(tmp_path):
+    """The verifier must reject when the mounted volume's name is not
+    'Plow' — guards against someone parameterizing -volname during build."""
+    result = _run_verifier_with_fake_hdiutil(
+        tmp_path, mount_basename="NotPlow", stage_volume_icon=False,
+    )
+    assert result.returncode != 0, (
+        f"verifier accepted DMG with wrong volume name: "
+        f"stdout={result.stdout!r} stderr={result.stderr!r}"
+    )
+    assert "expected 'Plow'" in result.stderr
+

+def test_just_dmg_verify_recipe_is_thin_alias_to_verifier(tmp_path):
+    """`just app dmg-verify` is the public no-arg entrypoint; it must be a
+    pass-through to plowd-verify-dmg, with no extra flags or wrapping that
+    would land it on a different code path than the inline release-script
+    call. We assert the recipe body forwards positional args verbatim and
+    does not pin a flag like `--dmg`."""
+    just_text = (REPO_ROOT / "app" / "justfile").read_text()
+    # Pull out the dmg-verify recipe block (header line + indented body).
+    match = re.search(
+        r"^dmg-verify[^\n]*:\n((?:    [^\n]*\n)+)",
+        just_text,
+        re.MULTILINE,
+    )
+    assert match is not None, "dmg-verify recipe not found in app/justfile"
+    body = match.group(1)
+    assert "plowd-verify-dmg" in body
+    # Round-3 collapse: the recipe must not pin --dmg or any other flag —
+    # one positional pass-through, same code path as the inline release-
+    # script call.
+    assert "--dmg" not in body, (
+        f"dmg-verify recipe still passes --dmg; should be a positional "
+        f"pass-through. Recipe body:\n{body}"
+    )

 def _fake_hdiutil_script() -> str:
     return """#!/usr/bin/env python3
 import hashlib
 import json
 import os
 from pathlib import Path
 import shutil
 import sys
 
 
 log_dir = Path(os.environ["FAKE_LOG_DIR"])
 map_path = log_dir / "hdiutil-map.json"
 if map_path.exists():
     image_map = json.loads(map_path.read_text())
 else:
     image_map = {}
 
 
 def save_map() -> None:
     map_path.write_text(json.dumps(image_map))
 
 
 def image_dir_for(image_path: str) -> Path:
     digest = hashlib.sha256(image_path.encode()).hexdigest()
     return log_dir / "images" / digest
 
 
 def copy_tree(src: Path, dest: Path) -> None:
     if dest.exists():
         shutil.rmtree(dest)
     dest.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     shutil.copytree(src, dest, symlinks=True)
 
 
 def find_value(flag: str, args: list[str]) -> str:
     return args[args.index(flag) + 1]
 
 
 with (log_dir / "hdiutil.log").open("a") as fh:
     fh.write(" ".join(sys.argv[1:]) + "\\n")
 
 command = sys.argv[1]
 args = sys.argv[2:]
 
 if command == "create":
     srcfolder = Path(find_value("-srcfolder", args))
     output = Path(args[-1])
     output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     output.write_text("fake dmg")
     captured = log_dir / "captured-srcfolder"
     copy_tree(srcfolder, captured)
     image_dir = image_dir_for(str(output))
     copy_tree(srcfolder, image_dir)
     image_map[str(output)] = str(image_dir)
     save_map()
     sys.exit(0)
 
 if command == "attach":
     image = next(arg for arg in args if not arg.startswith("-"))
-    mount_dir = Path("/Volumes") / f"fake-{hashlib.sha256(image.encode()).hexdigest()[:12]}"
+    digest = hashlib.sha256(image.encode()).hexdigest()[:12]
+    # Mount under FAKE_LOG_DIR (not /Volumes) so it is writable on every CI
+    # platform and so plowd-verify-dmg can inspect the mount via real
+    # filesystem reads. The basename "Plow" is what the verifier asserts on.
+    mount_dir = log_dir / "mounts" / digest / "Plow"
+    if mount_dir.exists():
+        shutil.rmtree(mount_dir)
+    source_dir_str = image_map.get(image)
+    if source_dir_str and Path(source_dir_str).exists():
+        copy_tree(Path(source_dir_str), mount_dir)
+    else:
+        mount_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     image_map[f"mount::{mount_dir}"] = image
     save_map()
     print(f"/dev/disk9s1 Apple_APFS {mount_dir}")
     sys.exit(0)
 
 if command == "detach":
     mount_dir = Path(args[0])
+    if str(mount_dir).startswith(str(log_dir)) and mount_dir.exists():
+        shutil.rmtree(mount_dir, ignore_errors=True)
     sys.exit(0)
 
 if command == "convert":
     source_image = next(arg for arg in args if not arg.startswith("-"))
     output = Path(find_value("-o", args))
     output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     output.write_text("fake compressed dmg")
     source_dir = Path(image_map[source_image])
     output_dir = image_dir_for(str(output))
     copy_tree(source_dir, output_dir)
     image_map[str(output)] = str(output_dir)
     save_map()
     sys.exit(0)
 
 if command == "info":
     sys.stdout.write(os.environ.get("FAKE_HDIUTIL_INFO", ""))
     sys.exit(0)
 
 sys.exit(0)
 """
 
 
 def _write_fake_container_build_commands(fake_bin: Path, build_log: Path) -> None:

   build) exit 0 ;;
   save) printf 'saved %s\\n' "$2"; exit 0 ;;
 esac
 exit 1
 """
         ),
         encoding="utf-8",
     )
     docker.chmod(0o755)

         textwrap.dedent(
             """#!/usr/bin/env bash

   case "$1" in
     -o) output="$2"; shift 2 ;;
     *) shift ;;
   esac
 done

 cat > "$output"
 """
         ),
         encoding="utf-8",
     )
     zstd.chmod(0o755)

     just_stub.chmod(0o755)

     6	## Active Scripts
     7	
     8	- `plowd-package-runtime`
     9	  - Syncs a staged runtime payload into `Plow.app`.
    10	  - Intended for local packaging/release assembly workflows.
    11	
    12	- `plowd-package-sparkle-update`
    13	  - Archives a signed `Plow.app` into a Sparkle-friendly ZIP update artifact.
    14	  - Use after the final app bundle has been signed.
    15	
    16	- `plowd-stage-sparkle-feed`
    17	  - Packages a `Plow.app` bundle and generates a local `appcast.xml`.
    18	  - Use this to stage a non-prod or prod Sparkle feed directory before upload.
    19	
    20	- `plowd-publish-sparkle-feed`
    21	  - Publishes a staged Sparkle feed to explicit S3 keys without deleting unrelated files.
    22	  - Used for production appcast/archive uploads.
    23	
    24	- `plowd-promote-release`
    25	  - Promotes a versioned release to the stable DMG and appcast keys.
    26	  - Use this after validation to make a packaged release visible to users.
    27	
    28	- `plowd-stage-runtime`
    29	  - Assembles bundled runtime under `app/plowd/runtime/stage`.
    30	  - Installs pinned Python + locked PlowD deps + stages OpenClaw assets from `app/openclaw/`.
    31	
    32	- `plowd-fetch-runtime-artifacts`
    33	  - Downloads pinned Node/OpenClaw artifacts into `app/plowd/runtime/artifacts`.
    34	  - Can write SHA256 values back into `app/plowd/runtime/manifest.toml`.
    35	
    36	- `plowd-validate-package`
    37	  - Validates packaged runtime end-to-end (`offline` or `online` mode).
    38	  - Checks bundle layout, launch source, and bundled CLI wiring.
    39	
    40	- `plowd-packaged-agent`
    41	  - Runs bundled OpenClaw CLI from a packaged `Plow.app`.
    42	  - Requires `PLOWD_OPENCLAW_ROOT_DIR` to point at the active bundle-scoped OpenClaw root, for example `~/Library/Application Support/<bundle-id>/openclaw`.
    43	
    44	- `plowd-tail-logs`
    45	  - Tails app/plowd/vm/openclaw logs with source filtering and timestamps.
    46	
    47	## Removed From This Folder

Recommended release order:

1. build signed `Plow.app`
2. `just app release`
   - uploads immutable versioned artifacts only:
   - `downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg`
   - `updates/Plow-<version>-<build>.zip`
   - `appcasts/Plow-<version>-<build>.xml`
3. optional local/manual validation
4. `just app promote <version> <build>`
   - updates stable pointers:
   - `Plow.dmg`
   - `appcast.xml`

## Current Scripts

Updater release scripts already in the repo:

- `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-package-sparkle-update`
- `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-stage-sparkle-feed`
- `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-publish-sparkle-feed`
- `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-promote-release`

These handle:

- packaging a full Sparkle ZIP
- generating a staged appcast
- publishing explicit Sparkle feed files to S3

exec
/bin/bash -lc "sed -n '120,180p' docs/distribution/CODE_SIGNING.md" in /tmp/tmp.VfFEF4WmXb/repo
 succeeded in 0ms:
Default output:

- `.build/Plow.dmg`
- `.build/Plow.dmg.sha256`

The command uploads versioned artifacts to S3:

- `s3://releases.plow.co/downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg`
- `s3://releases.plow.co/downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg.sha256`

The release rebuilds and repackages local runtime/VM assets into the app bundle, but does **not** publish runtime artifacts to S3 or rewrite the committed `runtime-manifest.json`. Runtime artifacts are managed separately via `just app runtime`.

## Validation Notes

The release script treats these as the important success signals:

- `codesign --verify --deep --strict` passes on the staged app before DMG creation
- Apple notarization status is `Accepted`
- `xcrun stapler staple` succeeds on the DMG

The script also performs a local `spctl --assess --type open` check on the DMG, but that check is advisory only. On some machines, `spctl` can be noisy or context-sensitive for DMGs even when notarization and stapling succeeded.

## Overrides

If needed, you can still override the defaults:

```bash
just app release notary_profile=my-profile s3_bucket=my-bucket
```

Or call the script directly:

```bash
app/plowd/scripts/plowd-beta-package-signed --identity "Developer ID Application: Your Name (TEAMID)"
```

Use an explicit `--identity` only if auto-detection picks the wrong certificate.

exec
/bin/bash -lc "sed -n '200,235p' docs/vm-publish.md" in /tmp/tmp.VfFEF4WmXb/repo
 succeeded in 0ms:
1. checks out `main`
2. verifies the two runtime S3 keys from `app/vm/manifest.toml`
3. runs `cd app && just release`
4. creates a versioned DMG and appcast
5. drafts a GitHub release tagged `deploy/app/v<version>-build.<build>`

`just release` does **not** upload runtime OCI tarballs. It only:

- regenerates `runtime-manifest.json` from `app/vm/manifest.toml`
- packages the signed/notarized app
- uploads the versioned DMG and appcast for that app release

The runtime artifact upload must already have happened before this point.

## Step 7: Promote the Published App Release

Publishing the GitHub draft release triggers `promote-app.yml`, which runs `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-promote-release`.

That script copies:

- `downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg` to `Plow.dmg`
- `downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg.sha256` to `Plow.dmg.sha256`
- `appcasts/Plow-<version>-<build>.xml` to `appcast.xml`

This promotion step affects the app installer/update feed only. It does **not** touch runtime OCI tarballs under `runtime/`.

## Verification Checklist

After `just runtime build`:

- `app/vm/manifest.toml` has the expected artifact names, shas, sizes, and git refs
- `app/Phoenix/Resources/runtime-manifest.json` matches the TOML entries
- both tarballs exist under `app/vm/output/`

After `just runtime deploy`:


codex
## [architecture] findings

### Surveyed
- Release packaging path in `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-beta-package-signed` — clean; it removes the UDRW/convert/FinderInfo branch and creates the shipping ULFO DMG directly.
- Mandatory post-staple verifier before S3 upload — clean; current branch has one release path, with no `PLOW_SKIP_DMG_VERIFY` or test-only bypass.
- `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-verify-dmg` as the artifact contract boundary — clean; the separate script keeps the release invariant reusable by both `just app dmg-verify` and the packaging script.
- Finder layout handling via checked-in `.DS_Store` plus `plowd-record-dmg-layout` — clean; the interactive authoring workflow is kept out of unattended CI/release packaging.
- macOS CI coverage for Darwin-only `hdiutil` behavior — clean; it extends the existing macOS app job rather than adding a parallel release architecture.
- PLO-29 spirit-vs-implementation — clean; the PR removes the custom volume-icon special case while preserving the stable “Plow” volume name and adding a final artifact guard without introducing a new product-facing distribution path.
